FROM (
    SELECT TOP(@__p_0) [b].[ScheduleId], [b].[BroadcastDate], [b].[EmployeeId], [b].[RecordId]
    FROM [BroadcastSchedule] AS [b]
) AS [b0]
INNER JOIN [Employees] AS [e] ON [b0].[EmployeeId] = [e].[EmployeeId]
INNER JOIN [Records] AS [r] ON [b0].[RecordId] = [r].[RecordId]

FROM (
    SELECT TOP(@__p_0) [b].[ScheduleId], [b].[BroadcastDate], [b].[EmployeeId], [b].[RecordId]
